{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01RaXP5bmXKWyv1h53JmtEyt","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_0121qX3LoQgfkMoimhjkoYSP","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/PLUGIN_VALIDATION_IMPLEMENTATION.md","content":"# Plugin Identifier Validation Implementation\n\n## Overview\n\nThis document describes the implementation of validation for plugin identifiers in NodeBB's plugin activation system.\n\n## Problem Statement\n\nNodeBB's plugin activation system processes malformed plugin identifiers without proper validation. Any string is accepted as a plugin identifier, including names with whitespace, special characters, or incorrect formats. Administrators receive no feedback when providing incorrect plugin names, making it difficult to identify errors.\n\n## Solution\n\nA validation function has been implemented in `/app/src/plugins/install.js` that checks plugin identifiers against established naming patterns before allowing them to be activated, installed, or queried.\n\n## Technical Details\n\n### Validation Logic\n\nThe validation function `validatePluginId(id)` performs three checks:\n\n1. **Type and emptiness check**: Ensures the identifier is a non-empty string\n   - Error: `[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]`\n\n2. **Whitespace check**: Rejects identifiers containing spaces, tabs, newlines, or other whitespace\n   - Error: `[[error:plugin-id-cannot-contain-whitespace]]`\n\n3. **Format check**: Validates against the established `pluginNamePattern` regex\n   - Pattern: `/^(@[\\w-]+\\/)?nodebb-(theme|plugin|widget|rewards)-[\\w-]+$/`\n   - Error: `[[error:plugin-id-invalid-format]]`\n\n### Valid Plugin Identifier Formats\n\nThe following formats are now accepted:\n- `nodebb-plugin-{name}` - Standard plugins\n- `nodebb-theme-{name}` - Themes\n- `nodebb-widget-{name}` - Widgets\n- `nodebb-rewards-{name}` - Rewards packages\n- `@scope/nodebb-plugin-{name}` - Scoped plugins\n\nExample valid identifiers:\n- `nodebb-plugin-markdown`\n- `nodebb-plugin-my-awesome-plugin`\n- `nodebb-theme-lavender`\n- `nodebb-widget-essentials`\n- `@nodebb/nodebb-plugin-abc`\n\n### Functions with Validation\n\nThe following functions now validate plugin identifiers at entry:\n\n1. `Plugins.toggleActive(id)` - Activate/deactivate plugins\n2. `Plugins.toggleInstall(id, version)` - Install/uninstall plugins\n3. `Plugins.upgrade(id, version)` - `[[error:plugin-id-invalid-format]]`\n\n### Valid Plugin Identifier Formats\n\nThe following formats are now accepted:\n- `nodebb-plugin-{name}` - Standard plugins\n- `nodebb-theme-{name}` - Themes\n- Error('[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]');\n    }\n\n    // Check 2: No whitespace\n    if (/\\s/.test(id)) {\n        throw new Error('[[error:plugin-id-cannot-contain-whitespace]]');\n    }\n\n    // Check 3: Matches naming pattern\n    if (!pluginNamePattern.test(id)) {\n        throw new Error('[[error:plugin-id-invalid-format]]');\n    }\n}\n```\n\n## Plugin Pattern\n\nThe validation uses the established pattern from `src/constants.js`:\n\n```regex\n^(@[\\w-]+\\/)?nodebb-(theme|plugin|widget|rewards)-[\\w-]+$\n```\n\nThis pattern accepts:\n- Optional scoped packages: `@scope/`\n- Required prefix: `nodebb-`\n- Required type: `theme`, `plugin`, `widget`, or `rewards`\n- Required suffix: `-{alphanumeric-and-hyphens}`\n\n## Functions Protected\n\nAll plugin activation/management functions Standard plugins\n- `nodebb-theme-{name}` - Themes\n- `nodebb-widget-{name}` - Widgets\n- `nodebb-rewards-{name}` - Rewards packages\n- `@scope/nodebb-{type}-{name}` - Scoped packages\n\n### Examples of Valid Identifiers\n```\nnodebb-plugin-markdown\nnodebb-plugin-my-awesome-plugin\nnodebb-theme-lavender\nnodebb-widget-essentials\n@nodebb/nodebb-plugin-abc\n```\n\n### Invalid Identifiers (All Rejected)\n```\n\" nodebb-plugin-test\"    ❌ Leading whitespace\n\"nodebb-plugin test\"     ❌ Space in middle\n\"my-plugin\"              ❌ No nodebb prefix\n\"nodebb-invalid-test\"    ❌ Invalid type\n\"nodebb-plugin-test@\"    ❌ Special character\n```\n\n## Functions Protected\n\nThe following plugin management functions now validate identifiers:\n\n1. `Plugins.toggleActive(id)` - Activate/deactivate plugins\n2. `Plugins.toggleInstall(id, version)` - Install/uninstall plugins\n3. `Plugins.upgrade(id, version)` - Upgrade plugins\n4. `Plugins.isInstalled(id)` - Check installation status\n5. `Plugins.isActive(id)` - Check activation status\n6. `Plugins.checkWhitelist(id, version)` - Validate against whitelist\n7. `Plugins.suggest(pluginId, nbbVersion)` - Get suggestions\n\n## Error Messages\n\nThree distinct error types are used for clear feedback:\n\n| Error | Condition |\n|-------|-----------|\n| `[[error:invalid-plugin-id]]` | Null, empty, or non-string identifier |\n| `[[error:plugin-id-cannot-contain-whitespace]]` | Identifier contains whitespace |\n| `[[error:plugin-id-invalid-format]]` | Identifier doesn't match naming pattern |\n\n## Success Criteria -
